**说明：**
<small>1. 本词汇表按分类及自然顺序而不是字母顺序排序。</small>
<small>2. 除了语辅词外，一般不标词性，因为可以从词尾判断词性。</small>
<small>3. 用<英语|法语|拼音>的格式标出词源；“-”号表示该种词源无。</small>
<small>4. 法语词源位置可能来自其他罗曼语，用[es]、[it]等标出。</small>
<small>5. 在基本词小节出现的复合词，词源格式标为< = >。</small>
<small>7. 由主词汇衍生出来的词条用“^►◊♦”符号引领。</small>
<small>8. 目前版本：V0.8；词汇完成度：80%；语辅词、基本词基本完成。</small>
## 语辅词
#### 人称代词
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>mo</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < me | moi | wo > </small></i>&nbsp; [代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 我 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | vous | ni > </small></i>&nbsp; [代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 你 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < you | vous | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 您 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>lu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | lui | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 他/她/它 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ilu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < it | il | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 他 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>elu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < she | elle | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 她 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ta</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < it | ça | ta > </small></i>&nbsp; [代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 它（无主代词/从句代词） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>moj</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 我们 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vij</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 你们 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>luj</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 他们/她们/它们 </p><p>&nbsp</p> 
#### 物主代词（绝对形式同形）
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>moe</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [代形/代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 我的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vie</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [代形/代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 你的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vue</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [代形/代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 您的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>lue</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [代形/代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 他的/她的/它的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ilue</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [代形/代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 他的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>elue</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [代形/代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 她的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>moje</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [代形/代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 我们的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vije</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [代形/代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 你们的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>luje</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [代形/代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 他们的/她们的/它们的 </p><p>&nbsp</p> 
#### 反身代词
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>seu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < self | se | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 自己，自身 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>moeseu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 我自己 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vieseu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 你自己 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vueseu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 您自己 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>lueseu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 他自己/她自己/它自己 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ilueseu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 他自己 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>elueseu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 她自己 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>mojeseu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 我们自己 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vijeseu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 你们自己 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>lujeseu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 他们/她们/它们自己 </p><p>&nbsp</p> 
#### 指代词
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>la</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < the | la | na > </small></i>&nbsp; [代形]&nbsp;&nbsp; 这/那，相当于英法的定冠词 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>zit</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < this | cette | zhe > </small></i>&nbsp; [代形/代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 这，这个 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>zij</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < these | ces | zheji > </small></i>&nbsp; [代形/代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 这些，这几个 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>zir</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < here | ici | zher > </small></i>&nbsp; [代副]&nbsp;&nbsp; （在）这里，这儿 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nat</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < that | cela | na > </small></i>&nbsp; [代形/代名/连]&nbsp;&nbsp; 那，那个；以至于... </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>naj</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < those | ces | naji > </small></i>&nbsp; [代形/代名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 那些，那几个 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nar</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < there | là | nar > </small></i>&nbsp; [代副]&nbsp;&nbsp; （在）那里，那儿 </p><p>&nbsp</p> 
#### 连词
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>e</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | et | he > </small></i>&nbsp; [连]&nbsp;&nbsp; 和，与；而且，并且 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>or</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < or | ou | huo > </small></i>&nbsp; [连]&nbsp;&nbsp; 或，或者 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sif</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < if | si | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [连]&nbsp;&nbsp; 如果；假如 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kos</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < cause | parceque | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [连]&nbsp;&nbsp; 因为 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>so</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < so | - | suo > </small></i>&nbsp; [连]&nbsp;&nbsp; 所以，因此 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>zen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < then | - | ran > </small></i>&nbsp; [连]&nbsp;&nbsp; 然后；那么 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kuaki</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [连]&nbsp;&nbsp; 虽然，尽管（“爱啥啥，爱谁谁”） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>mer</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | mais | er > </small></i>&nbsp; [连]&nbsp;&nbsp; 但是，然而 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | pendant | dang > </small></i>&nbsp; [连]&nbsp;&nbsp; 当...的时候 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sins</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < since | - | zi > </small></i>&nbsp; [连]&nbsp;&nbsp; 自...以来，自从... </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tis</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < till | - | zhi > </small></i>&nbsp; [连]&nbsp;&nbsp; 直到 </p><p>&nbsp</p> 
#### 介词
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>a</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < at | à | zai > </small></i>&nbsp; [介]&nbsp;&nbsp; 在…位置（时间、地点） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>in</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < in | en | li > </small></i>&nbsp; [介]&nbsp;&nbsp; 在…里面（时间、地点） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>am</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < on | en [es] | shang > </small></i>&nbsp; [介]&nbsp;&nbsp; 在…上面；在...方向 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < to | - | qu > </small></i>&nbsp; [介]&nbsp;&nbsp; 向，朝，去；(带动名词短语）去...，对于...，为了... </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>de</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | de | de > </small></i>&nbsp; [介]&nbsp;&nbsp; 的，属于…的；有关...的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>prev</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [介]&nbsp;&nbsp; 在…之前（时间） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>post</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [介]&nbsp;&nbsp; 在…之后（时间） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fron</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < from | - | cong > </small></i>&nbsp; [介]&nbsp;&nbsp; 从；自从 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dur</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < during | durant | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [介]&nbsp;&nbsp; 在…期间（时间） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bai</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < by | par | bei > </small></i>&nbsp; [介]&nbsp;&nbsp; 被；通过（方法，手段） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vis</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < with | avec | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [介]&nbsp;&nbsp; 以，凭，用；与…一起 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>as</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < as | - | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [介]&nbsp;&nbsp; 像…一样，跟…一样，如同 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>abu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < about | sur | yu > </small></i>&nbsp; [介]&nbsp;&nbsp; 关于，对于，至于；大约 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>zan</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < than | - | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [介]&nbsp;&nbsp; 比，相比 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>for</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < for | pour | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [介]&nbsp;&nbsp; 为，为了；由于 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>plus</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < plus | plus | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [介]&nbsp;&nbsp; 加，加上；正 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>minus</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < minus | moins | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [介]&nbsp;&nbsp; 减，减去；负 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>timis</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < times | fois | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [介]&nbsp;&nbsp; 乘，乘以 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>divis</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < divided by | divisé par | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [介]&nbsp;&nbsp; 除，除以 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>paus</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < power | pouvoir | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [介]&nbsp;&nbsp; 乘方，...次方，...次幂 </p><p>&nbsp</p> 
#### 疑问词
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ka</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | est-ce que | ma > </small></i>&nbsp; [疑副]&nbsp;&nbsp; 是...吗？是不是？（一般疑问词） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kua</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < what | quoi | sha > </small></i>&nbsp; [疑名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 啥？什么？(what) </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>forkua</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [疑连]&nbsp;&nbsp; 为啥？为什么？(why) </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ki</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | qui | shei > </small></i>&nbsp; [疑名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 谁？(who) </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kie</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp; [疑形]&nbsp;&nbsp; 谁的？(whose） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kui</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < which | qui | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [疑形/疑名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 哪个？那个 (which) </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kuen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < when | quand | shijian > </small></i>&nbsp; [疑副]&nbsp;&nbsp; 什么时间？（when） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kuer</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < where | - | nar > </small></i>&nbsp; [疑副]&nbsp;&nbsp; 什么地点？哪里？（where) </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>komen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | comment | zen > </small></i>&nbsp; [疑副]&nbsp;&nbsp; 怎么？怎样？（how） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>komoche</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | combien | duo > </small></i>&nbsp; [疑形]&nbsp;&nbsp; 多少？几多？(how much) </p><p>&nbsp</p> 
#### 语法副词
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>viam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < will | vien | hui > </small></i>&nbsp; [副]&nbsp;&nbsp; 将会，将，会 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>deja</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | déjà | yijing > </small></i>&nbsp; [副]&nbsp;&nbsp; 已经，已 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>jen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < -ing | - | zheng > </small></i>&nbsp; [副]&nbsp;&nbsp; 正在，在 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>si</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | si | shi > </small></i>&nbsp; [副]&nbsp;&nbsp; 是，是的；就，就是（肯定词，前后一致） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ne</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < not | ne | mei > </small></i>&nbsp; [副]&nbsp;&nbsp; 不，不是；没，没有（否定词，前后一致） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>alon</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < always | toujours | zong > </small></i>&nbsp; [副]&nbsp;&nbsp; 总是，永远（加强肯定） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>jame</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < never | jamais | bie > </small></i>&nbsp; [副]&nbsp;&nbsp; 从不，永不（加强否定） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>suvam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < often | souvent | chang > </small></i>&nbsp; [副]&nbsp;&nbsp; 常常，经常 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < now | maintenant | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [副]&nbsp;&nbsp; 现在，立刻，马上 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sun</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < soon | - | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [副]&nbsp;&nbsp; 即将，很快，不久 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>osie</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < also | aussi | ye > </small></i>&nbsp; [副]&nbsp;&nbsp; 也，也是，也这样 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>jait</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < yet | - | hai > </small></i>&nbsp; [副]&nbsp;&nbsp; 还是，仍然 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>onli</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < only | - | zhi > </small></i>&nbsp; [副/形]&nbsp;&nbsp; 只是，只有，仅仅；唯一 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>su</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < such | si | ru > </small></i>&nbsp; [副/形]&nbsp;&nbsp; 如此，这么，那么 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>even</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < even | - | shen > </small></i>&nbsp; [副]&nbsp;&nbsp; 甚至，更甚 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tren</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | très | hen > </small></i>&nbsp; [副]&nbsp;&nbsp; 很，非常 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tro</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < too | trop | guo > </small></i>&nbsp; [副]&nbsp;&nbsp; 过...，过于...，太... </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>mor</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < more | - | duo > </small></i>&nbsp; [副/形]&nbsp;&nbsp; 更（多，比较级），多一些 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>most</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < most | - | duo > </small></i>&nbsp; [副/形]&nbsp;&nbsp; 最（多，最高级） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>les</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < less | - | shao > </small></i>&nbsp; [副/形]&nbsp;&nbsp; 更（少，比较级），少一些 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>lest</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < least | - | shao > </small></i>&nbsp; [副/形]&nbsp;&nbsp; 最（少，最高级） </p><p>&nbsp</p> 
#### 情态副词
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vud</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < would | vouloir | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [情副]&nbsp;&nbsp; 愿意，想要 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kud</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < could | pouvoir | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [情副]&nbsp;&nbsp; 可以，能够（有能力或被允许） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>duad</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < ought | devoir | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [情副]&nbsp;&nbsp; 应该，必须 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>shud</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < should | - | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [情副]&nbsp;&nbsp; 就该，蛮好（虚拟语气） </p><p>&nbsp</p> 
#### 数词
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>zero</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < zero | zéro | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [数]&nbsp;&nbsp; 零 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>un</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < one | un | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [数/代]&nbsp;&nbsp; 一；某人，一个人 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>du</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < two | deux | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [数]&nbsp;&nbsp; 二 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tri</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < three | trois | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [数]&nbsp;&nbsp; 三 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fua</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < four | quatre | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [数]&nbsp;&nbsp; 四 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>cink</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < cinque | cinq | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [数]&nbsp;&nbsp; 五 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sis</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < six | six | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [数]&nbsp;&nbsp; 六 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sep</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < seven | sept | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [数]&nbsp;&nbsp; 七 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ok</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < oct- | oct- | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [数]&nbsp;&nbsp; 八 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nof</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < nine | neuf | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [数]&nbsp;&nbsp; 九 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dek</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < deca | deca | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [数]&nbsp;&nbsp; 十 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>cento</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < cent | cent | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [数]&nbsp;&nbsp; 百 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kilo</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < kilo | kilo | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [数]&nbsp;&nbsp; 千 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>milo</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < million | million | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [数]&nbsp;&nbsp; 兆，百万 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>gigo</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < giga | giga | ji > </small></i>&nbsp; [数]&nbsp;&nbsp; 吉，千兆，十亿 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tero</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < tera | tera | tai > </small></i>&nbsp; [数]&nbsp;&nbsp; 太，兆兆，万亿 </p><p>&nbsp</p> 
#### 叹词
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>halo</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < hello | hola [es] | hao > </small></i>&nbsp; [叹名]&nbsp;&nbsp; 哈罗！嗨！你好！（打招呼） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ah</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < alas | hélas | a > </small></i>&nbsp; [叹]&nbsp;&nbsp; 啊！哎！（感叹或悲伤） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>aha</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < aha | aha | ha > </small></i>&nbsp; [叹]&nbsp;&nbsp; 哈！（高兴,惊讶） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>oh</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < oh | ohlala | wo > </small></i>&nbsp; [叹]&nbsp;&nbsp; 喔！（明白）；喔？（疑问） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ops</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < ops | oups | - > </small></i>&nbsp; [叹]&nbsp;&nbsp; 哎呦！哎呀！（出错了） </p><p>&nbsp</p><p>&nbsp</p> 
## 基本名词
#### 天文地理
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vakon</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < vacumm | vacuum | kong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 空，真空，虚空 <br> ▹ <b>vakonz</b> &nbsp; 抽空，排空；真空吸尘<br> ▹ <b>vakonje</b> &nbsp; 空的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>universu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < universe | univers | yu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 宇宙；世界 <br> ▹ <b>universuje</b> &nbsp; 宇宙的；广泛的，普遍的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>matu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < matter | matière | wu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 物质；事物；事情 <br> ▹ <b>matuje</b> &nbsp; 物质的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>metin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < metal | metal | jin > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 金（金属） <br> ▹ <b>metinje</b> &nbsp; 金属性的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vudu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < wood | - | mu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 木 <br> ▹ <b>vuduje</b> &nbsp; 木属性的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>akui</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < aqua | acqua [it] | shui > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 水 <br> ▹ <b>akuiz</b> &nbsp; 融化，熔化，化成水；使熔化<br> ▹ <b>akuije</b> &nbsp; 水属性的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>firo</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < fire | feu | huo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 火 <br> ▹ <b>firoz</b> &nbsp; 起火，点火；开枪，开炮<br> ▹ <b>firoje</b> &nbsp; 火属性的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ertu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < earth | terre | tu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 土，土壤，泥土 <br> ▹ <b>ertuz</b> &nbsp; 腐烂，化成土；使腐烂<br> ▹ <b>ertuje</b> &nbsp; 土属性的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>stoni</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < stone | - | shi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 石，石头，岩石 <br> ▹ <b>stonije</b> &nbsp; 石头般的，硬的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sanda</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < sand | sable | sha > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 沙，沙子，砂砾 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pauden</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < powder | poudre | fen > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 粉，粉尘 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>cindui</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < cinder | cendre | hui > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 灰，灰尘，尘土 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>spacon</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < space | espace | kong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 空间，太空 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>starin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < star | star | xing > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 星球（统称），天体；恒星；明星 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>planin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < planet | planète | xing > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 行星 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>satelin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < satellite | satellite | xing > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 卫星 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>soli</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < solar | soleil | ri > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 日，太阳；阳光 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>lunue</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < lunar | lune | yue > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 月，月亮；月光 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>globi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < globe | globe | di > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 地，地球；地球仪 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>skian</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < sky | - | tian > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 天，天空 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>airi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < air | air | qi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 气，空气，大气 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>klimatou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < climate | climat | hou > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 气<候> </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tempi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < temper | temps | qi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 天<气>；脾气 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nuajun</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | nuage | yun > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 云 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>venton</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < vent- | vent | feng > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 风 <br> ▹ <b>ventonz</b> &nbsp; 起风，刮风</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>plu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < plumber | pluie | yu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 雨 <br> ▹ <b>pluz</b> &nbsp; 下雨</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tonei</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < thunder | tonnerre | lei > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 雷 <br> ▹ <b>toneiz</b> &nbsp; 打雷</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>elektian</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < electricity | electricité | dian > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 电 <br> ▹ <b>elektianz</b> &nbsp; 闪电<br> ▹ <b>elektianje</b> &nbsp; 电的，电动的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>snue</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < snow | neige | xue > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 雪 <br> ▹ <b>snuez</b> &nbsp; 下雪</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>glacin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < glacial | glace | bing > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 冰 <br> ▹ <b>glacinz</b> &nbsp; 结冰</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>frosuam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < frost | - | shuang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 霜 <br> ▹ <b>frosuamz</b> &nbsp; 结霜</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dulu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < dew | - | lu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 露 <br> ▹ <b>duluz</b> &nbsp; 结露</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fogu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < fog | - | wu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 雾 <br> ▹ <b>foguz</b> &nbsp; 起雾</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>smokian</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < smoke | - | yan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 烟 <br> ▹ <b>smokianz</b> &nbsp; 冒烟；抽烟，吸烟</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>stormon</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < storm | tormenta [es] | feng > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 风暴，暴风雨 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tornadon</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < tornado | tornade | feng > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 龙卷风 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>hurikon</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < hurricane | hurricane | feng > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 飓风 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>taifon</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < typhoon | typhon | feng > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 台风 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>landi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < land | - | di > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 地，陆地；土地；地盘；地区 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>plintelandi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 平原，平地 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>hautelandi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 高原，高地 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>montan</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < mount | mont | shan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 山，山峦，山峰，山丘 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sumon</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < summit | sommet | feng > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 峰，山峰，山顶；峰会 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>valu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < valley | vallée | gu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 谷，山谷 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>foren</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < forest | forêt | sen > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 森林 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>deso</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < desert | désert | mo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 漠，沙漠，大漠 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ociam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < ocean | océan | yang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 洋，大洋 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sai</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < sea | - | hai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 海，海洋 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>riveu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < river | rivière | he > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 河，河流，江 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>strimi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < stream | - | xi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 溪，溪流，小河 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kuriou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < current | courant | liu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 流，水流，气流，电流 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>branchi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < branch | branche | zhi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 支流；分支；树枝 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>laku</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < lake | lac | hu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 湖，湖泊 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>etam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | étang | tang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 塘，池塘 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sorcuan</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < source | source | quan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 泉，源泉；源头，来源；资源 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ilau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < island | île | dao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 岛，海岛，岛屿 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kostan</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < coast | costa [es] | an > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 岸，河岸，海岸 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>guan</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < gulf | golfe | wan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 湾，海湾 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>plajan</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < plage | plage | tan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 滩，沙滩，海滩 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>straitia</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < strait | stretto [it] | xia > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 峡，海峡 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>olam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | ola [es] | lang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 浪，波浪，波，水波 <br> ▹ <b>olamz</b> &nbsp; 波动；挥手</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>flian</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < flame | flamme | yan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 焰，火焰 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sisoni</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < season | saison | ji > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 季，季节 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>spun</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < spring | printemps | chun > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 春，春季，春天 <br> ▹ <b>spunje</b> &nbsp; 春天的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sumia</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < summer | - | xia > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 夏，夏季，夏天 <br> ▹ <b>sumiaje</b> &nbsp; 夏天的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>autiou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < autumn | automne | qiu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 秋，秋季，秋天 <br> ▹ <b>autiouje</b> &nbsp; 秋天的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vinton</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < winter | - | dong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 冬，冬季，冬天 <br> ▹ <b>vintonje</b> &nbsp; 冬天的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>timi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < time | temps | shi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 时间；时代；次数；倍数 <br> ▹ <b>timije</b> &nbsp; 适时的；及时的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dati</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < date | date | ri > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 日期；日子；年份，年代 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>anian</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < annual | an | nian > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 年，年份 <br> ▹ <b>anianje</b> &nbsp; 按年的，每年的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>montue</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < month | mois | yue > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 月，月份 <br> ▹ <b>montueje</b> &nbsp; 按月的，每月的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vikou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < week | - | zhou > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 周，星期 <br> ▹ <b>vikouje</b> &nbsp; 按周的，每周的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dian</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < day | date | tian > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 天，日，旦；白天 <br> ▹ <b>dianje</b> &nbsp; 按天的，每天的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nie</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < night | noir | ye > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 夜，晚，晚上 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>maten</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < morning | matin | chen > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 早<晨> </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>evan</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < evening | - | wan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 傍<晚>，晚上 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>hauri</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < hour | heure | shi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 时，小时；点钟 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>minuten</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < minute | minute | fen > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 分，分钟 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sekiau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < second | seconde | miao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 秒，秒钟 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>placi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < place | place | di > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 地方，地点 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vistin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < vista | vista [es] | jing > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 景观，风景 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>direktam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < direction | direction | xiang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 方向；方位 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>eston</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < east | est | dong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 东，东方，东边，东部 <br> ▹ <b>estonje</b> &nbsp; 东方的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sudan</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < south | sud | nan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 南，南方，南边，南部 <br> ▹ <b>sudanje</b> &nbsp; 南方的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vesti</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < west | ouest | xi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 西，西方，西边，西部 <br> ▹ <b>vestije</b> &nbsp; 西方的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nordei</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < north | nord | bei > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 北，北方，北边，北部 <br> ▹ <b>nordeije</b> &nbsp; 北方的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>midon</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < middle | milieu | zhong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 中，中间，中部 <br> ▹ <b>midonje</b> &nbsp; 中间的，其间的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>upam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < up | - | shang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 上，上方，上面，上部 <br> ▹ <b>upamje</b> &nbsp; 上面的；向上的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>undia</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < under | - | xia > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 下，下方，下面，下部 <br> ▹ <b>undiaje</b> &nbsp; 下面的；向下的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>lefto</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < left | - | zuo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 左，左方，左边 <br> ▹ <b>leftoje</b> &nbsp; 左边的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>raitiou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < right | droite | you > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 右，右方，右边 <br> ▹ <b>raitiouje</b> &nbsp; 右边的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>frian</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < front | front | qian > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 前，前方，前边 <br> ▹ <b>frianje</b> &nbsp; 前面的，前方的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bakou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < back | - | hou > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 后，后方，后边；后背 <br> ▹ <b>bakouje</b> &nbsp; 后面的，后方的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ini</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < inside | intérieur | li > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 里，里面 <br> ▹ <b>inije</b> &nbsp; 里面的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>autuai</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < outside | autre | wai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 外，外面 <br> ▹ <b>autuaije</b> &nbsp; 外面的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kotam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | côté | pang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 旁，旁边 <br> ▹ <b>kotamje</b> &nbsp; 旁边的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>korno</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < corner | coin | luo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 角<落> <br> ▹ <b>kornoje</b> &nbsp; 角落的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>topin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < top | - | ding > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 顶，顶部 <br> ▹ <b>topinje</b> &nbsp; 顶上的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>centon</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < center | centre | zhong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 中，正中，中点 <br> ▹ <b>centonje</b> &nbsp; 正中的，中央的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>boti</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < bottom | - | di > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 底，底部 <br> ▹ <b>botije</b> &nbsp; 底下的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>basi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < base | base | ji > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 基，基础；地基 <br> ▹ <b>basije</b> &nbsp; 基础的，基本的</p><p>&nbsp</p> 
#### 自然世界
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nati</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < nature | nature | zi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 自然，大自然；本性，本质 <br> ▹ <b>natije</b> &nbsp; 自然的，本性的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>specon</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < species | espèce | zhong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 种类，物种；类别 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bio</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < bio- | bio- | huo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 活体；生物 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vitin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < vita | vie | ming > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 生<命>；寿命；生活 <br> ▹ <b>vitinz</b> &nbsp; 怀孕，孕育，形成生命<br> ▹ <b>vitinje</b> &nbsp; 生命的，有生命的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>orguan</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < organ | organe | guan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 器官，组织 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>planti</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < plant | plante | zhi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 植物 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tru</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < tree | - | shu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 树 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ruten</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < root | - | gen > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 根 <br> ▹ <b>rutenz</b> &nbsp; 生根</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>stin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < stem | - | jing > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 茎，干；词干 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>folie</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < foli- | feuille | ye > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 叶，树叶；页，书页 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>flaura</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < flower | fleur | hua > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 花 <br> ▹ <b>flauraz</b> &nbsp; 开花；绽放（blossom）<br> ▹ <b>flauraje</b> &nbsp; 花一样的，如花似玉的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fruito</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < fruit | fruit | guo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 果，果实，水果 <br> ▹ <b>fruitoz</b> &nbsp; 结果；收获</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>budia</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < bud | bouton | ya > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 芽 <br> ▹ <b>budiaz</b> &nbsp; 发芽</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tran</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < trunk | tronc | gan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 干，主干；树干；躯干 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>grasau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < grass | - | cao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 草；草坪 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>apin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < apple | pomme | ping > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 苹果 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>piri</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < pear | poire | li > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 梨 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>oranjen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < orange | orange | cheng > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 橙子 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pichau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < peach | pêche | tao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 桃子 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bananau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < banana | le banane | jiao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 香蕉 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>melua</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < melon | melon | gua > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 瓜 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sidon</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < seed | - | zhong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 种子 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>binou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < bean | - | dou > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 豆，黄豆，大豆 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < pea | pois | dou > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 豌豆，小豆子 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nuto</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < nut | noix | guo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 坚果，果仁；螺母 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pounuto</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 花生（像豌豆一样的坚果） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kokonuto</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 椰子，椰果 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>soliflaura</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 向日葵，太阳花 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>juci</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < juice | jus | zhi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 汁液，果汁 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>animon</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < animal | animal | dong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 动物 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>biau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < bird | oiseau | niao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 鸟，雀，禽 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bistou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < beast | bête | shou > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 兽，野兽 <br> ▹ <b>bistouje</b> &nbsp; 野蛮的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fishu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < fish | - | yu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 鱼 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>insekon</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < insect | insecte | chong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 昆虫 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>veron</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < worm | ver | chong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 虫，蠕虫，线虫 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bugon</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < bug | bogue | chong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 臭虫，害虫；错误，缺陷 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>chiki</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < chicken | - | ji > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 鸡，鸡肉 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dukia</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < duck | carnad | ya > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 鸭，鸭肉 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>guseu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < goose | oie | e > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 鹅 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>chevala</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < chevalier | cheval | ma > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 马 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>boviniou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < bovine | bovin | niu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 牛，牛肉 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>mutam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < mutton | mouton | yang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 羊，羊肉 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>porku</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < porc | porc | zhu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 猪，猪肉 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dogou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < dog | - | gou > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 狗 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>katau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < cat | chat | mao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 猫 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>mausu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < mouse | souris | shu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 鼠，老鼠；鼠标 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>egan</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < egg | - | dan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 蛋；卵 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>milkai</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < milk | - | nai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 奶；牛奶 <br> ▹ <b>milkaije</b> &nbsp; 牛奶般的，丝滑的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bodi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < body | - | ti > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 体，躯体，躯干，身体，尸体 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fleshou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < flesh | - | rou > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 肉，肉体，果肉 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>cheva</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | cheveu | fa > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 发，毛发，头发 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pieli</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < pelt | piel [es] | pi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 皮，皮肤 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>furau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < fur | fourrure | mao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 毛，皮毛；毛皮 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>grisi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < grease | graisse | zhi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 脂，脂肪；肥肉；动物油 <br> ▹ <b>grisije</b> &nbsp; 油腻的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>blodue</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < blood | - |  > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 血，血液 <br> ▹ <b>blodueje</b> &nbsp; 血腥的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vein</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < vein | veine | jing > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 静脉；血管 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>arteron</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < artery | artère | dong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 动脉；主干，干流 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pulso</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < pulse | pulso [es] | bo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 脉<搏>，脉冲；跳动；冲动 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nervin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < nerve | nerf | jing > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 神<经>；经脉 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>musi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < muscle | muscle | ji > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 肌，肌肉，肉组织 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bonu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < bone | - | gu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 骨，骨头 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tetou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < head | tête | tou > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 头 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>brainau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < brain | - | nao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 脑，大脑 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>facian</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < face | face | lian > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 脸 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ian</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < eye | œil | yan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 眼 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pupon</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < pupil | pupille | tong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 瞳孔 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tirei</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < tear | - | lei > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 泪，眼泪 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>eur</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < ear | oreille | er > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 耳朵 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nosi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < nose | nez | bi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 鼻 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>gorgou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < gorge | gorge | hou > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 喉 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>mausou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < mouth | bouche | kou > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 口，嘴 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tongeu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < tonge | langue | she > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 舌 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>denti</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < dent- | dent | chi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 齿，牙，牙齿 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>javeu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < jaw | - | he > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 颌，下颌，颌骨；下巴 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>chineu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < chin | - | ke > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 颏，下颏，下巴 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>barbu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < barb | barbe | xu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 须，胡须，胡子 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nekin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < neck | nuque | jing > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 颈，脖子 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>chestion</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < chest | - | xiong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 胸 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bru</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < breast | - | ru > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 乳房 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>belu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < belly | - | fu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 腹，肚子 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>hartam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < heart | cœur | zang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 心，心脏 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>lungam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < lung | - | zang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 肺 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>stomam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < stomach | estomac | zang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 胃 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>livam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < liver | - | zang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 肝，肝脏 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kidnam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < kidney | - | zang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 肾，肾脏 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>intestinam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < intestine | intestin | zang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 肠子 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bladam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < bladder | - | zang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 膀胱 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vaistiau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < waist | - | yao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 腰，腰部 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>hipun</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < hip | hanche | tun > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 臀，臀部 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tailui</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < tail | - | wei > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 尾，尾巴 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>shoudian</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < shoulder | épaule | jian > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 肩，肩膀 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>manou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < mannual | main | shou > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 手 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>armi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < arm | arme | bi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 臂，手臂 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ristuan</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < wrist | - | wan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 腕，手腕 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < palm | paume | zhang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 掌，手掌 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fistuan</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < fist | - | quan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 拳，拳头 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fingi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < finger | - | zhi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; <i><small> < foot | - | zu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 足，脚 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>legui</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < leg | jambe | tui > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 腿；大腿 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kni</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < knee | - | xi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 膝，膝盖，膝关节 <br> ▹ <b>kniz</b> &nbsp; 用膝盖顶；跪，跪下（en: kneel）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ankuai</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < ankl | - | huai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 踝，脚踝，踝关节 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>talon</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | talon | zhong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 踵，脚后跟 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>orti</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | orteil | zhi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 趾，脚趾 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fungu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < fungus | fungo | gu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 蘑<菇>，菌菇；真菌，菌类 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>baktun</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < bacteria | bactérie | jun > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 细<菌> </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>viru</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < virus | virus | du > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 病<毒> </p><p>&nbsp</p> 
#### 材料工具
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>materiau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < material | matériel | liao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 料，材料，物料，物质，物品 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>goudin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < gold | or | jin > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 金，黄金；金色 <br> ▹ <b>goudinje</b> &nbsp; 金色的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>arjin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < argent | argent | yin > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 银，白银；银色；银子，钱 <br> ▹ <b>arjinje</b> &nbsp; 银色的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bron</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < bronze | bronze | tong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 铜，青铜；铜色，古铜色 <br> ▹ <b>bronje</b> &nbsp; 铜色的，古铜色的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fie</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < Fe | fer | tie > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 铁，铸铁；铁青色 <br> ▹ <b>fieje</b> &nbsp; 铁青色的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tini</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < tin | étain | xi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 锡；罐头 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>stilam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < steel | - | gang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 钢，钢铁 <br> ▹ <b>stilamz</b> &nbsp; 钢化，硬化<br> ▹ <b>stilamje</b> &nbsp; 钢铁般的，坚硬的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>plombian</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < Pb | plomb | qian > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 铅 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>merkuri</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < mercury | mercure | yin > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 水<银> </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>alin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < alloy | alliage | jin > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 合<金> </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>korku</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < cork | corcho [es] | mu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 软<木>；软木塞 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>leteu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < leather | - | ge > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 皮<革> </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>cementi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < cement | ciment | ni > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 水<泥> </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>klu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < clay | - | tu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 黏<土>，泥土 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>konkru</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < concrete | - | tu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 混凝<土>，凝结物 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>glasi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < glass | glace | li > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 玻<璃>；玻璃杯 <br> ▹ <b>glasije</b> &nbsp; 玻璃般的，透明的，晶莹剔透</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>rubiau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < rubber | - | jiao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 橡<胶>；橡皮 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tarin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < tar | - | qing > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 沥<青> </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>limui</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < nail | - | ding > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 钉子 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>skrin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < screw | - | ding > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 线，棉线；线索；细丝 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>lian</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < line | ligne | xian > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 线；路线；连线；队列，排 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>filmo</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < film | filme [pt] | mo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 膜，薄膜；胶片，电影 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>iou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < oil | huile | you > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 油（统称）；石油，原油；食用油 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>gasiou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < gas | gas | you > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 汽油 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>disiou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < diesel | diesel | you > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 柴油 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>karbei</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < coal | charbon | mei > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 煤，煤炭 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tulu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < tool | outil | ju > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 工<具>，用具；手段 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>hosuan</b>&nbsp; 绳索 <br> ▹ <b>ropenje</b> &nbsp; 绳子状的，蛇形的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nuam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < net | - | wang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 网；网络 <br> ▹ <b>nuamz</b> &nbsp; 网住；罩住<br> ▹ <b>nuamje</b> &nbsp; 网状的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ladi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < ladder | - | ti > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 梯子 <br> ▹ <b>ladije</b> &nbsp; 梯子装的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>eskalati</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < escalator | escalier | ti > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 楼<梯>；扶梯 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>elevati</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < elevator | élévateur | ti > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 电<梯>；升降机 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>hukou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < hook | - | gou > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 钩子；鱼钩 <br> ▹ <b>hukouz</b> &nbsp; 把...弯成钩形；钩住；钓鱼<br> ▹ <b>hukouje</b> &nbsp; 钩形的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pompen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < pump | pompe | beng > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 泵；水泵；气泵 <br> ▹ <b>pompenz</b> &nbsp; 泵；抽水；打气</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>peni</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < pen | penna [it] | bi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 笔；钢笔 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>penci</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < pencil | - | bi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 笔，铅笔；蜡笔 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>choki</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < chalk | craie | bi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 笔，粉笔 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>brushua</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < brush | brosse | shua > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 刷子；画笔；毛笔 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>gliao</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < glue | - | jiao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 胶水 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>inko</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < ink | encre | mo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 墨水 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ruli</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < ruler | règle | chi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 尺子 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pinen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < pin | épingle | zhen > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 针，别针，大头针 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>belin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < bell | - | ling > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 铃，铃铛；钟，钟型物 <br> ▹ <b>belinz</b> &nbsp; 响铃，摇铃</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>klokon</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < clock | - | zhong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 钟 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vachau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < watch | - | biao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 表，手表 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bateri</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < battery | batterie | chi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 电池 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>parasan</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < parasol | parasol | shan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 伞，雨伞，阳伞 </p><p>&nbsp</p> 
#### 人世百态
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>humen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < human | humain | ren > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 人，智人；人类（集合） <br> ▹ <b>humenje</b> &nbsp; 有人性的，人道的，仁慈的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pipen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < people | peuple | ren > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 人，人们；人民，群众（集合） <br> ▹ <b>pipenje</b> &nbsp; 人民的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>persen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < person | personne | ren > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; <i><small> < vegetable | végétal | cai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 菜（统称），蔬菜，素菜；青菜 <br> ▹ <b>vejetaiz</b> &nbsp; 炒菜，做菜<br> ▹ <b>vejetaije</b> &nbsp; 素的（食物）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>mitou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < meat | - | rou > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 肉，食用肉，果肉；荤菜 <br> ▹ <b>mitouje</b> &nbsp; 荤的（食物）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>steikai</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < steak | - | pai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 牛<排>；肉排；鱼排 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>butiou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < butter | beurre | you > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 黄<油> </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>krimiou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < cream | crème | you > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 奶<油> </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>chisau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < cheese | - | lao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 奶<酪>，干酪 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>hamou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < ham | jambon | rou > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 腌<肉>，火腿 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sausajam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < sausage | saucisse | chang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 香<肠>，腊肠 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>onion</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < onion | oignon | cong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 洋<葱>；葱 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tomatie</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < tomato | tomate | qie > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 番<茄>，西红柿 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sala</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < salad | salade | la > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 沙拉，色拉 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>supam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < soup | la soupe | tang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 汤 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>toufu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < tofu | tofu | fu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 豆腐 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>jinjam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < ginger | gingembre | jiang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 姜 <br> ▹ <b>jinjamje</b> &nbsp; 姜色的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>garluan</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < garlic | - | suan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 蒜 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>salian</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < salt | sal [es] | yan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 盐 <br> ▹ <b>salianje</b> &nbsp; 咸的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sociam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < sauce | sauce | jiang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 酱，酱油；调味汁 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>jam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < jam | - | jiang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; <i><small> < wine | vin | jiu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 酒，果酒；葡萄酒 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>biou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < beer | bière | jiu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; <i><small> < mustard | moutarde | jie > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 芥，芥末 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pepu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < pepper | poivre | hu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 饼干 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>chokoli</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < chocolate | chocolat | li(qiaokeli) > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 巧克力 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kafei</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < coffee | café | fei(kafei) > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 咖啡 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>cha</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | chá [pt] | cha > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; <i><small> < cigarette | cigarette | yan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 烟，香烟 </p><p>&nbsp</p> 
#### 文化文明
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kultua</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < culture | culture | hua > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 文<化> <br> ▹ <b>kultuaje</b> &nbsp; 文化的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>civilin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < civilization | civilisation | ming > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 文<明> <br> ▹ <b>civilinz</b> &nbsp; 使...文明；进步<br> ▹ <b>civilinje</b> &nbsp; 文明的，讲文明的，有素质的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>spiren</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < spirit | esprit | shen > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 精<神> <br> ▹ <b>spirenje</b> &nbsp; 精神的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>relijau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < religion | religion | jiao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 宗<教> <br> ▹ <b>relijauje</b> &nbsp; 宗教的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>goden</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < god | - | shen > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 神，（大写首字母）上帝，天主 <br> ▹ <b>godenje</b> &nbsp; 神圣的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ferian</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < fairy | fée | xian > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 仙，神仙；仙子，精灵 <br> ▹ <b>ferianje</b> &nbsp; 有仙气的，飘逸的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>devo</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < devil |  | mo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 魔，魔鬼 <br> ▹ <b>devoje</b> &nbsp; 邪恶的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>gostui</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < ghost | - | gui > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 鬼，鬼魂 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>churchau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < church | - | jiao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 教堂；教会，教派 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tempiau</b>&nbsp; 建国，立国<br> ▹ <b>kontroje</b> &nbsp; 国家的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>provincen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < province | province | sheng > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 省 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>statou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < state | état | zhou > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 州 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kontian</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < county | comte | xian > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 县 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vilajun</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < village | village | cun > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 村 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>citi</b>&nbsp;
