<i><small> < story | histoire | shi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 故<事> </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>novo</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < novel | novela [es] | shuo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 小<说> </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>movin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < movie | - | ying > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 电<影> </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>poetri</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < poetry | poésie | shi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 诗，诗歌 <br> ▹ <b>poetrije</b> &nbsp; 有诗意的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>arti</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < art | art | yi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 艺术，美术 <br> ▹ <b>artije</b> &nbsp; 艺术的；文艺的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dramu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < drama | dramu | ju > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 剧，戏剧，歌剧，舞剧 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>musue</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < music | musique | yue > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 乐，音乐 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>instrumi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < instrument | instrument | qi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 乐<器>；仪器 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pianin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < piano | piano | qin > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 钢<琴> </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>violin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < violin | violon | qin > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 提<琴> </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>gita</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < guitar | guitare | ta(jita) > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 吉<他> </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sporti</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < sport | sport | ti > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 体育，运动 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>gami</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < game | - | xi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 游<戏>，嬉戏 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < ball | balle | qiu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 球 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>konfu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < kung-fu | kung-fu | gongfu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 功夫 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>archon</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < arch | archet | gong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 弓 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>arian</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < arrow | - | jian > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 箭 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dartiau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < darts | - | biao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 镖，飞镖 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tentam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < tent | tente | zhang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 帐篷 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>cartu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < chart | carte | tu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 地<图> </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kompan</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < compass | compas | pan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 罗<盘>，指南针 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>chesi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < chess | échecs | qi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 棋 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dicou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < dice | dés | tou > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 骰子 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>militun</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < military | millitaire | jun > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 军事，军用；军队 <br> ▹ <b>militunje</b> &nbsp; 军事的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>armun</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < army | armée | jun > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 军队；陆军 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>armu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < arm | arme | wu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 武器，装备；武装；武力 <br> ▹ <b>armuz</b> &nbsp; 武装，装备</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>geran</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | guerre | zhan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 战争 <br> ▹ <b>geranz</b> &nbsp; 宣战</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>batan</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < battle | bataille | zhan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 战斗，战争 <br> ▹ <b>batanz</b> &nbsp; 战斗；斗争</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tankeu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < tank | tank | ke(tanke) > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 坦克；储罐，油箱，水箱 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>gam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < gun | - | qiang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 枪；手枪 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kanau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < cannon | cannon | pao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 炮，加农炮 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bulan</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < bullet | balle | dan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 弹，子弹，炮弹 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>histori</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < history | histoire | shi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 历史 <br> ▹ <b>historiz</b> &nbsp; 使成为历史，留名青史<br> ▹ <b>historije</b> &nbsp; 历史的，历史性的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>politen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < politics | politique | zheng > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 政治 <br> ▹ <b>politenz</b> &nbsp; 政治化<br> ▹ <b>politenje</b> &nbsp; 政治的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>filoseu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < philosophy | philosophie | zhe > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 哲理；道理 <br> ▹ <b>filoseuje</b> &nbsp; 哲学的；有哲理的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>lua</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < law | loi | fa > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 法律 <br> ▹ <b>luaz</b> &nbsp; 成为法律，法律化<br> ▹ <b>luaje</b> &nbsp; 法律的；合法的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ekonomin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < economy | économie | jin > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 经济 <br> ▹ <b>ekonominje</b> &nbsp; 经济的；节俭的，有效率的</p><p>&nbsp</p> 
#### 一般概念
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>chosu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | chose | shi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 物，事物，东西，存在；事情 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>objektu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < object | objet | wu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 物体；客体，目标；宾语 <br> ▹ <b>objektuje</b> &nbsp; 客观的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>solidu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < solid | solide | gu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 固体，固态 <br> ▹ <b>soliduz</b> &nbsp; 固化，凝固；使结实，使牢固<br> ▹ <b>soliduje</b> &nbsp; 固态的，稳固的，稳定的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>likuidie</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < liquid | liquide | ye > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 液体，液态 <br> ▹ <b>likuidiez</b> &nbsp; 液化，凝结；使液化，使凝结<br> ▹ <b>likuidieje</b> &nbsp; 液态的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>gasi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < gas | gaz | qi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 气体，气态 <br> ▹ <b>gasiz</b> &nbsp; 气化，蒸发；使气化，使蒸发<br> ▹ <b>gasije</b> &nbsp; 气态的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>forci</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < force | force | li > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 力，力量；武力，军队 <br> ▹ <b>forciz</b> &nbsp; 迫使<br> ▹ <b>forcije</b> &nbsp; 有力的，强有力的；有说服力的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pauri</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < power | pouvoir | li > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 力量，能力；功率；电力；权力 <br> ▹ <b>paurije</b> &nbsp; 有力量的；有权势的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>enerjen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < energy | énergie | neng > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 能量，能源 <br> ▹ <b>enerjenje</b> &nbsp; 精力旺盛的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>velocitu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < velocity | vitesse | su > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 速度 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sonen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < sonal | son | sheng > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 声音，声响 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>voicen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < voice | voix | sheng > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 声音，嗓音（说话或唱歌） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>noisen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < noise | - | sheng > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 噪<声>，噪音 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>toniau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < tone | ton | yin > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 音<调>；音色；色调 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>hiteu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < heat | - | re > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 热，热能，热量 <br> ▹ <b>hiteuz</b> &nbsp; 加热<br> ▹ <b>hiteuje</b> &nbsp; 热情的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>luam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < luminary | lumière | guang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 光，光源；灯；光明 <br> ▹ <b>luamz</b> &nbsp; 发光；点亮，点燃，点火<br> ▹ <b>luamje</b> &nbsp; 光明的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>shadin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < shadow | - | ying > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 影，影子 <br> ▹ <b>shadinz</b> &nbsp; 遮挡；使暗淡；使朦胧<br> ▹ <b>shadinje</b> &nbsp; 阴凉的；阴暗的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>coleu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < color | couleur | se > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 色，色彩，颜色 <br> ▹ <b>coleuz</b> &nbsp; 染色<br> ▹ <b>coleuje</b> &nbsp; 彩色的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>afairi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < affaire | affaires | shi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 事情，事务；生意（复） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fakti</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < fact | fait | shi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 事实 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>eventi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < event | événement | shi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 事件，活动 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>akcidi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < accident | accident | shi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 事故，意外 <br> ▹ <b>akcidije</b> &nbsp; 意外的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>disastai</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < disaster | désastre | zai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 灾难，灾祸 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kuestun</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < question | question | wen > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 问题 <br> ▹ <b>kuestunz</b> &nbsp; 提问</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>problan</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < problem | problème | nan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 难题，问题；课题 <br> ▹ <b>problanz</b> &nbsp; 出难题，难为，为难（tu … ）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>regui</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < regulation | règle | gui > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 规则；规律 <br> ▹ <b>reguije</b> &nbsp; 有规律的；常规的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ordu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < order | ordre | xu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 顺<序>，次序；秩序 <br> ▹ <b>orduz</b> &nbsp; 排序<br> ▹ <b>orduje</b> &nbsp; 有次序的；有秩序的；井井有条</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>risin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < reason | raison | yin > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 原<因>；理由（主观的） <br> ▹ <b>risinz</b> &nbsp; 合理化<br> ▹ <b>risinje</b> &nbsp; 有原因的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>resulto</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < result | résultat | guo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 结<果>（宽泛的） <br> ▹ <b>resultoz</b> &nbsp; 产生...结果</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kosin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < cause | causer | yin > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 因，原因，起因（客观的） <br> ▹ <b>kosinz</b> &nbsp; 导致，引起</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>efekto</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < effect | effet | guo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 果，结果，效果（具体的） <br> ▹ <b>efektoz</b> &nbsp; 产生...效果</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>endo</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < end | - | jie > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 末尾，结尾；末端，结束，死亡 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>disefekto</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 缺陷；缺点（意指效果被破坏） <br> ▹ <b>disefektoje</b> &nbsp; 有缺点的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>eru</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < error | erreur | wu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 误差，过失，错误 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>rogeo</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 错误，失误；罪过 <br> ▹ <b>rogeoje</b> &nbsp; 错误的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>krimui</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < crime | crime | zui > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 罪行，罪恶 <br> ▹ <b>krimuiz</b> &nbsp; 犯罪<br> ▹ <b>krimuije</b> &nbsp; 有罪的；罪恶的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sistemi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < system | système | xi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 体<系>，系统 <br> ▹ <b>sistemiz</b> &nbsp; 系统化<br> ▹ <b>sistemije</b> &nbsp; 系统化的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>relati</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < relation | relation | xi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 关<系>；联系 <br> ▹ <b>relatiz</b> &nbsp; 使...有联系/有关系<br> ▹ <b>relatije</b> &nbsp; 有关系的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sumarai</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < summary | - | gai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 概述，概要；总结 <br> ▹ <b>sumaraiz</b> &nbsp; 总结，概述<br> ▹ <b>sumaraije</b> &nbsp; 概要性的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>detaili</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < detail | détail | xi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 细节，细目，明细，详情 <br> ▹ <b>detailije</b> &nbsp; 细节化的，细致的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sampli</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < sample | - | yang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 样<例>，样品，样本，抽样 <br> ▹ <b>sampliz</b> &nbsp; 抽样</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>eksampi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < example | exemp | li > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 示<例>，例子；榜样 <br> ▹ <b>eksampiz</b> &nbsp; 示范</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ambiti</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < ambition | ambition | zhi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 志向，抱负；雄性；野心 <br> ▹ <b>ambitije</b> &nbsp; 有志向的，有抱负的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>festivie</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < festival | festival | jie > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 节日，节庆 <br> ▹ <b>festivieje</b> &nbsp; 节日的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vakatia</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < vacation | vacances | jia > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 假日 <br> ▹ <b>vakatiaz</b> &nbsp; 放假</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>chanci</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < chance | chance | ji > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 机会；时机 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fortun</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < fortune | fortune | yun > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 运气，幸运 <br> ▹ <b>fortunje</b> &nbsp; 幸运的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>metie</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | métier | ye > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 职<业>，工作 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>profesie</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < profession | profession | ye > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 专<业>，专业领域；职业 <br> ▹ <b>profesieje</b> &nbsp; 专业的；熟练的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>karie</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < career | carrière | ye > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 事<业>，职业 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tasku</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < task | tâche | wu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 任<务>；工作，差事 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>salarin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < salary | salaire | xin > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 薪金，薪酬，工资 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>revouzo</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 报酬；奖金，奖品 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>propertai</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < property | propriété | cai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 财产，不动产 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>richai</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | richesse | cai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 财富 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pricia</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < price | prix | jia > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 价格 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>valia</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < value | valeur | jia > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 价值 <br> ▹ <b>valiaje</b> &nbsp; 有价值的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>profi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < profit | profit | li > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 利润；利益 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>interu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < interest | intéresser | qu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 兴<趣>；利益；利息 <br> ▹ <b>interuz</b> &nbsp; 引起兴<趣>，使...感兴趣<br> ▹ <b>interuje</b> &nbsp; 有趣的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>debtai</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < debt | dette | zhai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 债务 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>akam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < account | - | zhang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 账户 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bilam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < bill | billet | zhang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 账单 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>chekiau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < cheque | chèque | piao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 支<票> </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tikiau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < ticket | ticket | piao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 票，入场券；罚单 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>taksui</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < tax | - | shui > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 税；费 <br> ▹ <b>taksuiz</b> &nbsp; 征税，收税</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>recitu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < receipt | reçu | ju > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 收<据>，凭据，回执 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>listie</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < list | liste | lie > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 列表，名单，清单 <br> ▹ <b>listiez</b> &nbsp; 列举，列表</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sumeu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < sum | somme | he > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 合计，累计，求和 <br> ▹ <b>sumeuz</b> &nbsp; 求和</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>degru</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < degree | degré | du > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 度，程度；等级；学位 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>skalu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < scale | échel | du > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 刻度，尺度；规模；天平 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>distancu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < distance | distance | ju > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 距离，间距 <br> ▹ <b>distancuje</b> &nbsp; 有距离的，遥远的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>siza</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < size | - | da > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 大小，尺寸 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>cikou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < cycle | cyclette | zhou > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 周期；循环 <br> ▹ <b>cikouje</b> &nbsp; 周期性的，循环的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>cikluan</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < circle | cercle | yuan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 圆，圆圈；圆周；循环 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tron</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < hole | trou | kong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 孔，洞 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>krosi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < cross | croix | shi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 十字，十字架；交叉 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sidian</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < side | côté | bian > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 边，面，侧面 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>angiau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < angle | ang | jiao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 角；角度 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bordian</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < border | bord | bian > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 边缘 <br> ▹ <b>bordianz</b> &nbsp; 边缘化<br> ▹ <b>bordianje</b> &nbsp; 边缘的，不重要的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>surfiau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < surface | surface | biao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 表面，表层 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>skin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < square | carré | pin > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 平方；方形；广场 <br> ▹ <b>skinz</b> &nbsp; 求平方</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kubi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < cube | cube | li > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 立方，立方体；骰子 <br> ▹ <b>kubiz</b> &nbsp; 求立方</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>averin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < average | - | ping > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 平均 <br> ▹ <b>averinz</b> &nbsp; 求平均；平均化<br> ▹ <b>averinje</b> &nbsp; 平均化的，平均的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kurvu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < curve | courbe | qu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 曲线 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>peram</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < pair | paire | shuang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 双，一双；副，对 <br> ▹ <b>peramz</b> &nbsp; 配对<br> ▹ <b>peramje</b> &nbsp; 成对的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>demi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 半，一半 <br> ▹ <b>demiz</b> &nbsp; 减半<br> ▹ <b>demije</b> &nbsp; 一半的，半个的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dropi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < drop | - | di > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 滴，一滴 <br> ▹ <b>dropiz</b> &nbsp; 滴下，滴落</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>hipui</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < heap | - | dui > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 堆，一堆 <br> ▹ <b>hipuije</b> &nbsp; 成堆的；很多的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pian</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < piece | pièce | pian > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 片，一片；片状物 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>futui</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < future | - | wei > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 未来，将来 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>crisui</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < crisis | crise | wei > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 危机，危险时刻 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>comitui</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < committee | comité | hui > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 委员<会> </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tritue</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < treaty | traité | yue > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 条<约>，契约，协议 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>prufen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < proof | preuve | zheng > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 证据 <br> ▹ <b>prufenz</b> &nbsp; 证明；提供证据<br> ▹ <b>prufenje</b> &nbsp; 有证据的，铁证如山</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>stepu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < step | passé | bu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 步子，步骤；脚步；台阶(复) <br> ▹ <b>prufenz</b> &nbsp; 迈步，往前走</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>jesti</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < gesture | geste | zi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 姿势 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>jokiau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < joke | - | xiao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 笑话，玩笑 <br> ▹ <b>stepuz</b> &nbsp; 开玩笑<br> ▹ <b>jokiauje</b> &nbsp; 好笑的，滑稽的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>metoda</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < method | méthode | fa > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 方<法>，办法，手段 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>artifi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < artifice | artifice | ji > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 诡<计>，计谋；技巧 <br> ▹ <b>artifije</b> &nbsp; 假的，人造的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kustu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < custom | coutume | su > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 风<俗>，民俗；习惯 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>riskian</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < risk | risque | xian > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 风<险>，危险 <br> ▹ <b>riskianje</b> &nbsp; 危险的，有风险的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>environmin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < environment | - | jing > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 环<境>；处境，外界，周围 </p><p>&nbsp</p><p>&nbsp</p> 
## 基本动词
#### 高频常用
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ez</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < is | es | shi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 是（性质状态）；在（位置）；被（表示被动） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>haz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < has | avoir | - > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 有，拥有；具有 <br> ▹ <b>hazo</b> &nbsp; 拥有；拥有的东西</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>doz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < do | - | zuo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 做，施行 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fuez</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < feel | - | jue > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 觉，觉得，感觉（系动词） <br> ▹ <b>fuezo</b> &nbsp; 感觉，直感</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>getenz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < get | - | cheng > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 成，变成，成为（系动词） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>siamz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < seem | sembler | xiang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 像，像是，好像（系动词） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>triz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < try | tratar [es] | shi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 试，尝试；考验；审判 <br> ▹ <b>trizo</b> &nbsp; 试验，尝试；审讯</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < want | vouloir | yao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 要，想要 <br> ▹ <b>vauzo</b> &nbsp; 愿望</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>doneiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < donate | donner | gei > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 给，给予，送给；赠予 <br> ▹ <b>doneizo</b> &nbsp; 赠送；赠品；礼品</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>takaz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < take | - | na > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 拿，拿走，取走；带去；服用 <br> ▹ <b>takazo</b> &nbsp; 收入，收获</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>aluz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | aller | qu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 去，过去 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>venaiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | venir | lai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 来，过来 </p><p>&nbsp</p> 
#### 基本动作
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tinz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < listen | écouter | ting > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 听，倾听（不涉及结果） <br> ▹ <b>tinzo</b> &nbsp; 听，倾听；所闻</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>soz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < say | - | shuo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 说，说话，说道 <br> ▹ <b>sozo</b> &nbsp; 说话；所说；言语；说法</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>duz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < read | - | du > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 读，阅读，看书 <br> ▹ <b>duzo</b> &nbsp; 阅读</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>riez</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < write | écrire | xie > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 写，写字，写作 <br> ▹ <b>riezo</b> &nbsp; 写作；作品</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kanz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < look | - | kan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 看，观看（不涉及结果） <br> ▹ <b>kanzo</b> &nbsp; 看；照看；所见；面容</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>smunz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < smell | sentir | wen > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 闻，嗅闻（不涉及结果） <br> ▹ <b>smunzo</b> &nbsp; 气味<br> ▹ <b>smunze</b> &nbsp; 有味道的，臭的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tuchoz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < touch | toucher | mo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 摸，触摸（不涉及结果） <br> ▹ <b>tuchozo</b> &nbsp; 触摸；触感</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tastamz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < taste | - | chang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 尝，品尝（不涉及结果） <br> ▹ <b>tastamzo</b> &nbsp; 品尝；口味，品味<br> ▹ <b>tastamze</b> &nbsp; 有品位的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tinauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < listen | écouter | tingdao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 听到，听见（有结果） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kanauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < look | - | kandao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 看到，看见（有结果） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tuchauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < touch | toucher | modao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 摸到（有结果） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>smunauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < smell | sentir | wendao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 闻到（有结果） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tastamauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < taste | - | changdao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 尝到（有结果） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tinaiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < listen | écouter | tingqilai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 听起来（系动词） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kanaiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < look | - | kanqilai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 看起来（系动词） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tuchaiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < touch | toucher | moqilai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 摸起来（系动词） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>smunaiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < smell | sentir | wenqilai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 闻起来（系动词） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tastamaiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < taste | - | changqilai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 尝起来，吃起来（系动词） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>rauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < run | courir | pao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 跑，跑步 <br> ▹ <b>rauzo</b> &nbsp; 跑步，跑步运动；奔跑</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tiauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | sauter | tiao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 跳，跳高 <br> ▹ <b>tiauzo</b> &nbsp; 跳跃</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fleiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < fly | - | fei > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 飞，飞翔 <br> ▹ <b>fleizo</b> &nbsp; 飞翔</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>najouz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | nager | you > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 游，游泳 <br> ▹ <b>najouzo</b> &nbsp; 游泳</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sitoz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < sit | - | zuo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 坐；坐落 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>stanz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < stand | - | zhan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 站，站立 <br> ▹ <b>stanzo</b> &nbsp; 站立；停留；站台</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kraz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < crawl | crawl | pa > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 爬，爬行 <br> ▹ <b>krazo</b> &nbsp; 爬行</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>marchouz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < march | marcher | zou > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 走，走路；散步 <br> ▹ <b>marchouzo</b> &nbsp; #### 生活社交
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vivoz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < vivid | vivre | huo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 活，生活 <br> ▹ <b>vivozo</b> &nbsp; 生活<br> ▹ <b>vivoze</b> &nbsp; 活的；生活的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>habuz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < inhabit | habiter | zhu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 住，居住 <br> ▹ <b>habuzo</b> &nbsp; 居住<br> ▹ <b>habuze</b> &nbsp; 居住的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>batuz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < bath | baigner | xi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 浴，沐浴，洗澡 <br> ▹ <b>batuzo</b> &nbsp; 洗澡；淋浴</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dormuiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < dormitive | dormir | shui > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 睡，睡觉 <br> ▹ <b>dormuizo</b> &nbsp; 瞌睡；觉<br> ▹ <b>dormuize</b> &nbsp; 瞌睡的，嗜睡的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>manjiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < manger | manger | chi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 吃，咀嚼 <br> ▹ <b>manjizo</b> &nbsp; 食物</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>drinz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < drink | - | he > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 喝，<饮> <br> ▹ <b>drinzo</b> &nbsp; 饮料，饮品<br> ▹ <b>drinze</b> &nbsp; 喝醉的，醉的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>eskraz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < excrete | excréter | la > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 拉，排泄，大便；疏散 <br> ▹ <b>eskrazo</b> &nbsp; 粪便</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pisaz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < piss | pisser | sa > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 撒，撒尿，小便 <br> ▹ <b>pisazo</b> &nbsp; 小便，尿</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kuisenz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < cuisine | cuisiner | peng > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 烹，烹饪 <br> ▹ <b>kuisenzo</b> &nbsp; 烹饪</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>frauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < fry | frire | chao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 炒，炒菜；煎，油炸 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>stenz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < steam | - | zheng > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 蒸，蒸煮 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>stunz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < stew |  | dun > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 炖，炖汤 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>toustauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < toast | arrosto [it] | kao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 烤，烧烤；烘，烘焙 <br> ▹ <b>toustauzo</b> &nbsp; 烧烤；烤肉</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vashiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < wash | - | xi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 洗，洗涤，冲洗 <br> ▹ <b>vashizo</b> &nbsp; 洗涤</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kombuz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < comb | - | shu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; #### 学习工作
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>edukiauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < educate | éduquer | jiao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 教，教育 <br> ▹ <b>edukiauzo</b> &nbsp; 教育</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tichauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < teach | - | jiao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 教，教书，教学 <br> ▹ <b>tichauzo</b> &nbsp; 教学</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>studuez</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < study | étudier | xue > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 学，学习，上学，念书；研究 <br> ▹ <b>studuezo</b> &nbsp; 学习；研究</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>lernuez</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < learn | - | xue > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 学，获得信息 <br> ▹ <b>lernuezo</b> &nbsp; 学习，模仿</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>spelinz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < spell | épeler | pin > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 拼写 <br> ▹ <b>spelinzo</b> &nbsp; 拼写</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>receiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < recite | réciter | bei > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 背诵，复述 <br> ▹ <b>receizo</b> &nbsp; 背诵</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kontuz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < count | compter | shu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; #### 认知感受
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kniz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < know | connaître | zhi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 知，知道 <br> ▹ <b>knizo</b> &nbsp; 知道；知识<br> ▹ <b>knize</b> &nbsp; 想象<br> ▹ <b>figamze</b> &nbsp; 想象中的，虚假的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>belivinz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < believe | - | xin > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 信，相信 <br> ▹ <b>belivinzo</b> &nbsp; <i><small> < Amor | amour | ai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 爱，喜欢 <br> ▹ <b>amaizo</b> &nbsp; 爱，热爱，爱戴</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>adonz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < adore | adorer | chong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; <i><small> < forget | - | wang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 忘记 <br> ▹ <b>forguamzo</b> &nbsp; 忘记</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>hesitiouz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < hesitate | hésiter | you > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 强调；强调点，重点</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>admireiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < admire | admirer | pei > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 佩服，钦佩；赞美 <br> ▹ <b>admireizo</b> &nbsp; 佩服；赞美</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>despiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < despise | despreciar [es] | bi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 鄙视，轻视，藐视 <br> ▹ <b>despizo</b> &nbsp; 鄙视</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>regriz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < regret | regretter | hui > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 悔，后悔；遗憾 <br> ▹ <b>regrizo</b> &nbsp; 后悔；遗憾<br> ▹ <b>regrize</b> &nbsp; 保证；保险<br> ▹ <b>asurauze</b> &nbsp; 保险的；确定的</p><p>&nbsp</p> 
#### 冲突变化
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>conflonz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < conflict | - | chong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 冲突；冲撞，抵触 <br> ▹ <b>conflonzo</b> &nbsp; 冲突<br> ▹ <b>conflonze</b> &nbsp; 毁灭<br> ▹ <b>destrize</b> &nbsp; 毁灭性的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>krakiez</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < crack | craquer | lie > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 裂开，破裂，碎裂；使破裂 <br> ▹ <b>krakiezo</b> &nbsp; 破裂；裂缝</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>damunz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < damage | endommager | sun > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 损坏，损毁，损害，伤害 <br> ▹ <b>damunzo</b> &nbsp; 损坏；损失</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>trituiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < threaten | - | wei > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 威胁，威吓，威慑 <br> ▹ <b>trituizo</b> &nbsp; 威胁<br> ▹ <b>trituize</b> &nbsp; 有威胁的，危险的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>persekoz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < persecute | persécuter | po > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 迫害；压迫 <br> ▹ <b>persekozo</b> &nbsp; 迫害；压迫</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>rubaz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < rub | frotter | ca > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 摩<擦>；惹怒 <br> ▹ <b>rubazo</b> &nbsp; 摩擦</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>iritiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < bury | - | mai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 埋葬 <br> ▹ <b>buraizo</b> &nbsp; 埋葬</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>blameuz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < blame | blâmer | zhe > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 训斥；批评</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>abuz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < abuse | - | ru > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 辱骂，侮辱；虐待；滥用 <br> ▹ <b>abuzo</b> &nbsp; 侮辱；虐待</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kouz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < curse | - | zhou > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 咒骂，诅咒 <br> ▹ <b>kouzo</b> &nbsp; 咒骂，诅咒；咒语</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>akuzianz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < accuse | accuser | qian > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 替，替换，代替，更换 <br> ▹ <b>replizo</b> &nbsp; 替换，更换</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>hapenz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < happen | - | sheng > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 生，发生 <br> ▹ <b>hapenzo</b> &nbsp; 弄<空>，使...空 <br> ▹ <b>emptonzo</b> &nbsp; 空虚<br> ▹ <b>emptonze</b> &nbsp; 空虚的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>asenz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < ascend | ascendre | sheng > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; #### 一般行为
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ekzaiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < exist | éxister | zai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 在，存在 <br> ▹ <b>ekzaizo</b> &nbsp; 存在；世间万物<br> ▹ <b>ekzaize</b> &nbsp; 存在的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kompiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < compare | comparer | bi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 比，比较 <br> ▹ <b>kompizo</b> &nbsp; 对比物；对比结果<br> ▹ <b>kompize</b> &nbsp; 对比的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>apartuz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < appertain | appartenir | shu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 属于 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>posesonz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < possess | posséder | yong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 拥有，持有，占有 <br> ▹ <b>posesonzo</b> &nbsp; 拥有；拥有物</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>uzonz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < use | employer | yong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 用，使用 <br> ▹ <b>uzonzo</b> &nbsp; 使用，用处；用法<br> ▹ <b>uzonze</b> &nbsp; 有用的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>aplonz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < apply | appliquer | yong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 用，应用，适用；涂敷（药物） <br> ▹ <b>aplonzo</b> &nbsp; 应用</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>aplenz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < apply | - | shen > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 申请 <br> ▹ <b>aplenzo</b> &nbsp; 申请；申请书</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>definz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < define | définir | ding > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 定义 <br> ▹ <b>definzo</b> &nbsp; 定义</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>reprezaiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < represent | représenter | dai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 代表 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>korespuz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < correspond | correspondre | fu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 符合 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>behinz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < behave | - | xing > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 行为；表现 <br> ▹ <b>behinzo</b> &nbsp; 表现，行为</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>prauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < pray | prier | dao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 祷告，祈祷，祈福 <br> ▹ <b>prauzo</b> &nbsp; 祈祷</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bluz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < bless | blesser | zhu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 祝福，保佑 <br> ▹ <b>bluzo</b> &nbsp; 保佑，祝福，福佑</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pasinz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < pass | passer | jing > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 经过，通过 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tranz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < trans- | traverser | chuan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 穿过；交叉，（使）相交 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>supeuz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < suppose | supposer | she > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 假<设>，假定 <br> ▹ <b>supeuzo</b> &nbsp; 假设；前提<br> ▹ <b>supeuze</b> &nbsp; 假设性的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pretuamz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < pretend | - | zhuang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 假<装> <br> ▹ <b>pretuamzo</b> &nbsp; 假装，伪装<br> ▹ <b>pretuamze</b> &nbsp; 虚假的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ekzajeraz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < exaggerate | exaggérer | kua > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 夸张，夸大 <br> ▹ <b>ekzajerazo</b> &nbsp; 夸张<br> ▹ <b>ekzajeraze</b> &nbsp; 夸张的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>deskriauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < describe | décrire | miao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 描述，描写，叙述 <br> ▹ <b>deskriauzo</b> &nbsp; 描写；叙述</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>imitoz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < imitate | imiter | mo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 模仿，仿效 <br> ▹ <b>imitozo</b> &nbsp; 模仿</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>grindoz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < grind | moudre | mo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 磨碎；折磨 <br> ▹ <b>grindozo</b> &nbsp; 折磨</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vandaiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < wander | - | pai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 徘徊，游荡 <br> ▹ <b>vandaizo</b> &nbsp; 徘徊</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>distinguz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < distinguish | distinguer | qu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 区别，区分 <br> ▹ <b>distinguzo</b> &nbsp; 区别，区别点</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>distribenz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < distribute | distribuer | fen > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 分布 <br> ▹ <b>distribenzo</b> &nbsp; 分布</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dispersanz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < disperse | disperser | san > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 散开，分散；散布；驱散 <br> ▹ <b>dispersanze</b> &nbsp; 分散的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>hidamz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < hide | - | cang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 藏匿，隐藏；掩藏 <br> ▹ <b>hidamzo</b> &nbsp; 隐藏</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>serchunz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < search | chercher | xun > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 寻找，搜索 <br> ▹ <b>serchunzo</b> &nbsp; 搜索</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kontonz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < contain | contenir | rong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 容纳 <br> ▹ <b>kontonzo</b> &nbsp; 容纳；内容</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>brakaz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < brake | - | sha > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 刹住，刹车 <br> ▹ <b>brakazo</b> &nbsp; 刹车，刹车片</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>omituez</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < omit | omettre | lue > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 略过，省略，忽略；遗漏 <br> ▹ <b>omituezo</b> &nbsp; 省略</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>remiouz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < remain | rester | liu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 留下，剩下 <br> ▹ <b>remiouzo</b> &nbsp; 遗留物</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vakinz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < waken | - | xing > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 唤<醒>，惊醒，使觉醒 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>surprizinz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < surprise | surprendre | jing > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 使<惊>奇 <br> ▹ <b>surprizinzo</b> &nbsp; 惊喜<br> ▹ <b>surprizinze</b> &nbsp; 令人惊奇的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>suficuz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < suffice | suffire | zu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 足够，使满足 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>adjusiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < adjust | ajuster | shi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 适应；适合 <br> ▹ <b>adjusizo</b> &nbsp; 适应</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>konvincoz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < convince | convaincre | shuo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 说服，使相信，使信服 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sanz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < sigh | soupirer | tan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 叹气，叹息 <br> ▹ <b>sanzo</b> &nbsp; 叹气，叹息</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dijauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < digest | digérer | xiao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 消化 <br> ▹ <b>dijauzo</b> &nbsp; 消化；文摘</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>extianz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < extend | étendre | yan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 延长 <br> ▹ <b>extianzo</b> &nbsp; 延长</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>delanz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < delay | - | yan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 延迟，延误 <br> ▹ <b>delanzo</b> &nbsp; 延误</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kuotinz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < quote | - | yin > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 引用 <br> ▹ <b>kuotinzo</b> &nbsp; 引用；引文</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>espanz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < expose | exposer | zhan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 展览，展出 <br> ▹ <b>espanzo</b> &nbsp; 展览</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>montrianz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < demonstrate | montrer | xian > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 显示，展示 <br> ▹ <b>montrianzo</b> &nbsp; 显示，展示</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>brilauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < brilliant | briller | zhao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 照耀，照亮 <br> ▹ <b>brilauzo</b> &nbsp; 照耀；光辉<br> ▹ <b>brilauze</b> &nbsp; 明亮的；光辉的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pleuz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < ply | plier | zhe > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 折叠 <br> ▹ <b>pleuzo</b> &nbsp; 折叠</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>provenz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < prove | prouver | zheng > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 证明 <br> ▹ <b>provenzo</b> &nbsp; 证明；证据</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dezerviz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < deserve | mériter | zhi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 值得 <br> ▹ <b>dezervize</b> &nbsp; 值得的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>indikiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < indicate | indiquer | zhi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 指示 <br> ▹ <b>indikizo</b> &nbsp; 指示，指令</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>repitonz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < repeat | répéter | chong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 重复 <br> ▹ <b>repitonzo</b> &nbsp; 重复<br> ▹ <b>repitonze</b> &nbsp; 重复性的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dekoranz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < decorate | décorer | zhuang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 装饰 <br> ▹ <b>dekoranzo</b> &nbsp; 装饰</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>prepeiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < prepare | préparer | bei > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 准<备> <br> ▹ <b>prepeizo</b> &nbsp; 准备；准备工作<br> ▹ <b>prepeize</b> &nbsp; 有准备的，准备好了的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>espraz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < express | - | da > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 表<达>，陈述，表示 <br> ▹ <b>esprazo</b> &nbsp; 表达，用语，语句</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kontaktuz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < contact | contacter | chu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 接<触>；联系 <br> ▹ <b>kontaktuzo</b> &nbsp; 接触；联系；联系人</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>orijinaiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < originate |  | lai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 来源于，起源 <br> ▹ <b>orijinaizo</b> &nbsp; 来源，起源；起点，原点</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>repauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < report | rapporter | bao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 报告；报道 <br> ▹ <b>repauzo</b> &nbsp; 报告，报道</p><p>&nbsp</p><p>&nbsp</p> 
## 基本形容词
#### 外观状态
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bone</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < bona | bonne | bang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 好，好的，棒的 <br> ▹ <b>boneo</b> &nbsp; 好事；好人</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>mave</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < mad | mauvaise | cha > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 坏，坏的，差的 <br> ▹ <b>maveo</b> &nbsp; 坏事；坏人</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>beile</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < belle | belle | mei > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 美，美丽，漂亮 <br> ▹ <b>beileo</b> &nbsp; 美丽；美丽的东西；美人<br> ▹ <b>beilez</b> &nbsp; 美化</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ougle</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < ugle | - | chou > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 丑，丑的，丑陋 <br> ▹ <b>ougleo</b> &nbsp; 丑陋；丑陋的东西；丑鬼<br> ▹ <b>ouglez</b> &nbsp; 丑化</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>lamge</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < long | long | chang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 长，长的，高的（人） <br> ▹ <b>lamgeo</b> &nbsp; 长度<br> ▹ <b>lamgez</b> &nbsp; 加长</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>shante</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < short | - | duan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 短，短的，矮的（人） <br> ▹ <b>shantez</b> &nbsp; 缩短</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>haute</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < high | haute | gao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 高，高的（位置） <br> ▹ <b>hauteo</b> &nbsp; 高度<br> ▹ <b>hautez</b> &nbsp; 增高</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>baise</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < base | basse | ai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 矮，低的（位置） <br> ▹ <b>baisez</b> &nbsp; 压低，降低</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vande</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < wide | - | kuan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 宽，宽的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>naire</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < narrow | - | zhai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 窄，窄的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>gronde</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < grand | grand | hong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 宏，宏大，宏伟，伟大，盛大 <br> ▹ <b>grondeo</b> &nbsp; 伟大；壮举，伟绩；伟人</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>jute</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < giant | - | ju > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 巨，巨大的，极大的 <br> ▹ <b>juteo</b> &nbsp; 巨人</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>larje</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < large | large | da > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 大，大的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>monde</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < medium | milieu | zhong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 中，中等的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>smiaule</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < small | - | xiao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 小，小的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tine</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < tiny | petit | xi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 细，细小的，微小的，袖珍的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>numore</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < numerous | numeroso [es] | duo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 多，很多的，许多的；大量的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>moche</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < much | mucho [es] | duo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 多，多的 <br> ▹ <b>mocheo</b> &nbsp; 大量</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>laute</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < little | - | shao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 少，少的 <br> ▹ <b>lauteo</b> &nbsp; 少量，少许，一点</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fauve</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < few | peu | shao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 少，很少的，极少的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>linge</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < light | ligero [es] | qing > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 轻的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>honve</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < heavy | - | zhong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 重的 <br> ▹ <b>honveo</b> &nbsp; 重量</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nonurjite</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 缓，不急的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>urjite</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < urgent | urgent | ji > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 急，紧急的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>taute</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | tôt | zao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 早的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>lante</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < late | - | wan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 晚的，迟的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kuaike</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < quick | - | kuai > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 快的 <br> ▹ <b>kuaikez</b> &nbsp; 加快</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>slane</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < slow | lent | man > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 慢的 <br> ▹ <b>slanez</b> &nbsp; 拖慢，阻止</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>strone</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < strong | foncèe | nong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 浓的（颜色） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>klane</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < clear | claire | dan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 淡的（颜色） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>douse</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < dense | denso [es] | chou > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 稠的，浓的（成分比例） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dilite</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < dilute | diluèe | xi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 稀的，淡的（成分比例） </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>grouse</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | grosse | hou > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 厚的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>mauce</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | mince | bao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 薄的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>denpe</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < deep | - | shen > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 深的 <br> ▹ <b>denpeo</b> &nbsp; 深邃，深沉；深度<br> ▹ <b>denpez</b> &nbsp; 加深，深化</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nondenpe</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 浅的 <br> ▹ <b>nondenpeo</b> &nbsp; 浅薄</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>suanfte</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < soft | - | ruan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 软的 <br> ▹ <b>suanftez</b> &nbsp; 软化</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>hinde</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < hard | - | yin > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 硬的 <br> ▹ <b>hindez</b> &nbsp; 硬化，加固</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>strite</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < straight | droite | zhi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 直的，笔直的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kurve</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < curved | courbe | qu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 曲的，弯曲的，曲折的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kamre</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < square | carré | fang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 方的 <br> ▹ <b>kamreo</b> &nbsp; 方形</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>rande</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < round | ronde | yuan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 圆的 <br> ▹ <b>randeo</b> &nbsp; 圆形，圆饼；小园片，垫圈</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>shanpe</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < sharp | tranchante | jian > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 尖的，尖锐的；锋利的 <br> ▹ <b>shanpeo</b> &nbsp; 尖儿<br> ▹ <b>shanpez</b> &nbsp; 削尖；磨锋利</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>blunte</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < blunt | - | dun > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 钝的，不锋利的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>stianke</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < sticky | - | nian > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 粘的，粘性的，粘乎乎的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>node</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < nude | desnudo [es] | luo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 裸的，裸体的；无装饰的；直率的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>raufe</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < rough | raboteuse | cao > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 糙的，粗糙的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>luase</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | lisse | hua > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 滑的，光滑的，平滑的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>suane</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < sour | - | suan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 酸的 <br> ▹ <b>suaneo</b> &nbsp; 酸；醋，醋酸；酸性物质</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dianse</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < - | douxe | tian > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 甜的 <br> ▹ <b>dianseo</b> &nbsp; 甜；糖</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bute</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < bitter | - | ku > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 苦的；涩的；苦涩的，难受的 <br> ▹ <b>buteo</b> &nbsp; 苦，苦闷，苦涩</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>spase</b>&nbsp; 绿色，绿色的东西</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>blane</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < blue | bleue | lan > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 蓝的 <br> ▹ <b>blaneo</b> &nbsp; 蓝色，蓝色的东西</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vile</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < violet | violette | zi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 紫的 <br> ▹ <b>vileo</b> &nbsp; 紫色，紫色的东西</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>rense</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < rose | rose | fen > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; #### 品质心态
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>able</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < able | capable | - > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 能的，有能力的 <br> ▹ <b>ableo</b> &nbsp; 能力</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>strame</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < strong | - | qiang > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 强的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>foble</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < feeble | faible | ruo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 弱的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>facile</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < facile | facile | yi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 易，容易的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nonfacile</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < = > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 难，困难的 <br> ▹ <b>nonfacileo</b> &nbsp; 困难，困难的事</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>intelije</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < intelligent | intelligent | zhi > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 智能的，智慧的；聪明的 <br> ▹ <b>intelijeo</b> &nbsp; 智能，智力<br> ▹ <b>intelijez</b> &nbsp; 智能化，使…智能</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vuize</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < wise | - | hui > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 智慧的 <br> ▹ <b>vuizeo</b> &nbsp; 智慧；智者</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>smonte</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < smart | smart | chong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 聪明的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vuale</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < wily | - | hua > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 滑头的，狡猾的，狡诈的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>stupende</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < stupid | stupide | ben > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 笨的，不聪明的 <br> ▹ <b>stupendeo</b> &nbsp; 笨拙；笨蛋，笨东西</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ridikunle</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < ridiculous | ridicule | chun > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 蠢的，愚蠢的 <br> ▹ <b>ridikunleo</b> &nbsp; 愚蠢；蠢人</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pinre</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < poor | pauvre | pin > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 贫困的，穷的 <br> ▹ <b>pinreo</b> &nbsp; 贫穷；穷人</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ruche</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < rich | riche | fu > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 富裕的，富的 <br> ▹ <b>rucheo</b> &nbsp; 富裕；富人</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bronve</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < brave | brave | yong > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 勇敢的，大胆的，无畏的 <br> ▹ <b>bronveo</b> &nbsp; 勇敢；勇士</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>timode</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < timid | timide | nuo > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 懦弱的，胆小的，畏惧的 <br> ▹ <b>timodeo</b> &nbsp; 胆怯；胆小鬼</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>polite</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < polite | polie | li > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 礼貌的 <br> ▹ <b>politeo</b> &nbsp; 饥饿</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>teuste</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < thirst | soif | ke > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 渴的，口渴的 <br> ▹ <b>teusteo</b> &nbsp; 口渴</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>donfe</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < deaf | - | long > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 聋的，有听力障碍的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>mate</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < mute | muette | ya > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 贪婪的，贪心的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>stinje</b>&nbsp; <i><small> < stingy | - | lin > </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp; 吝啬的，小气的；苛刻的 </p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>shoume</b>&nbsp;
